ARTICLES
--------


WINNING DECKS
=============





















Find out what’s been winning with this collection of top decks from recent Premier *Magic*.


For winning decks from the current Pro Tour Qualifier season, [click here](http://magic.wizards.com/en/articles/archive/fate-reforged-top-8-draft-decklists-2014-09-12).


For *Magic Online* winning decklists, [click here](http://magic.wizards.com/en/gameinfo/products/magiconline/decklists).
